\ifproblemToFind% If it has a desirable problem search the file.
%\tagged{Ans@ShortAns, Type@Compute, Topic@Derivative, Sub@Related-Rates, File@0031}{
\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Compute Question 0031. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

A road running north to south crosses a road going east to west at the point $P$.  Cyclist $A$ is riding north along the first road, and cyclist $B$ is riding east along the second road.  At a particular time, cyclist $A$ is ${15}$ ${\text{\texttt{thousand{ }feet}}}$ to the north of $P$ and traveling at ${36}$ ${\text{\texttt{feet{ }per{ }second}}}$, while cyclist $B$ is ${20}$ ${\text{\texttt{thousand{ }feet}}}$ to the east of $P$ and traveling at ${27}$ ${\text{\texttt{feet{ }per{ }second}}}$.  How fast is the distance between the two cyclists changing? \\[0.5in]

\input{Derivative-Compute-0031.HELP.tex}

The distance between the two cyclists is increasing by $\answer{\frac{216}{5}}$ ${\text{\texttt{feet{ }per{ }second}}}$.
\end{problem}}%}

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Compute Question 0031. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

A road running north to south crosses a road going east to west at the point $P$.  Cyclist $A$ is riding north along the first road, and cyclist $B$ is riding east along the second road.  At a particular time, cyclist $A$ is ${120}$ ${\text{\texttt{kilometers}}}$ to the north of $P$ and traveling at ${10}$ ${\text{\texttt{kilometers{ }per{ }hour}}}$, while cyclist $B$ is ${225}$ ${\text{\texttt{kilometers}}}$ to the east of $P$ and traveling at ${\frac{16}{3}}$ ${\text{\texttt{kilometers{ }per{ }hour}}}$.  How fast is the distance between the two cyclists changing? \\[0.5in]

\input{Derivative-Compute-0031.HELP.tex}

The distance between the two cyclists is increasing by $\answer{\frac{160}{17}}$ ${\text{\texttt{kilometers{ }per{ }hour}}}$.
\end{problem}}%}

At a particular time, cyclist $A$ is ${24}$ ${\text{\texttt{hundred{ }meters}}}$ to the north of $P$ and traveling at ${24}$ ${\text{\texttt{meters{ }per{ }second}}}$, while cyclist $B$ is ${32}$ ${\text{\texttt{hundred{ }meters}}}$ to the east of $P$ and traveling at ${18}$ ${\text{\texttt{meters{ }per{ }second}}}$.  How fast is the distance between the two cyclists changing? \\[0.5in]

\input{Derivative-Compute-0031.HELP.tex}

The distance between the two cyclists is increasing by $\answer{\frac{144}{5}}$ ${\text{\texttt{meters{ }per{ }second}}}$.
\end{problem}}%}

At a particular time, cyclist $A$ is ${96}$ ${\text{\texttt{miles}}}$ to the north of $P$ and traveling at ${45}$ ${\text{\texttt{miles{ }per{ }hour}}}$, while cyclist $B$ is ${180}$ ${\text{\texttt{miles}}}$ to the east of $P$ and traveling at ${24}$ ${\text{\texttt{miles{ }per{ }hour}}}$.  How fast is the distance between the two cyclists changing? \\[0.5in]

\input{Derivative-Compute-0031.HELP.tex}

The distance between the two cyclists is increasing by $\answer{\frac{720}{17}}$ ${\text{\texttt{miles{ }per{ }hour}}}$.
\end{problem}}%}

At a particular time, cyclist $A$ is ${8}$ ${\text{\texttt{miles}}}$ to the north of $P$ and traveling at ${30}$ ${\text{\texttt{miles{ }per{ }hour}}}$, while cyclist $B$ is ${15}$ ${\text{\texttt{miles}}}$ to the east of $P$ and traveling at ${16}$ ${\text{\texttt{miles{ }per{ }hour}}}$.  How fast is the distance between the two cyclists changing? \\[0.5in]

\input{Derivative-Compute-0031.HELP.tex}

The distance between the two cyclists is increasing by $\answer{\frac{480}{17}}$ ${\text{\texttt{miles{ }per{ }hour}}}$.
\end{problem}}%}

At a particular time, cyclist $A$ is ${70}$ ${\text{\texttt{miles}}}$ to the north of $P$ and traveling at ${18}$ ${\text{\texttt{miles{ }per{ }hour}}}$, while cyclist $B$ is ${168}$ ${\text{\texttt{miles}}}$ to the east of $P$ and traveling at ${\frac{15}{2}}$ ${\text{\texttt{miles{ }per{ }hour}}}$.  How fast is the distance between the two cyclists changing? \\[0.5in]

\input{Derivative-Compute-0031.HELP.tex}

The distance between the two cyclists is increasing by $\answer{\frac{180}{13}}$ ${\text{\texttt{miles{ }per{ }hour}}}$.
\end{problem}}%}

How fast is the distance between the two cyclists changing? \\[0.5in]

\input{Derivative-Compute-0031.HELP.tex}

The distance between the two cyclists is increasing by $\answer{\frac{240}{13}}$ ${\text{\texttt{kilometers{ }per{ }hour}}}$.
\end{problem}}%}

At a particular time, cyclist $A$ is ${65}$ ${\text{\texttt{hundred{ }meters}}}$ to the north of $P$ and traveling at ${48}$ ${\text{\texttt{meters{ }per{ }second}}}$, while cyclist $B$ is ${156}$ ${\text{\texttt{hundred{ }meters}}}$ to the east of $P$ and traveling at ${20}$ ${\text{\texttt{meters{ }per{ }second}}}$.  How fast is the distance between the two cyclists changing? \\[0.5in]

\input{Derivative-Compute-0031.HELP.tex}

The distance between the two cyclists is increasing by $\answer{\frac{480}{13}}$ ${\text{\texttt{meters{ }per{ }second}}}$.
\end{problem}}%}

At a particular time, cyclist $A$ is ${6}$ ${\text{\texttt{thousand{ }feet}}}$ to the north of $P$ and traveling at ${12}$ ${\text{\texttt{feet{ }per{ }second}}}$, while cyclist $B$ is ${8}$ ${\text{\texttt{thousand{ }feet}}}$ to the east of $P$ and traveling at ${9}$ ${\text{\texttt{feet{ }per{ }second}}}$.  How fast is the distance between the two cyclists changing? \\[0.5in]

\input{Derivative-Compute-0031.HELP.tex}

The distance between the two cyclists is increasing by $\answer{\frac{72}{5}}$ ${\text{\texttt{feet{ }per{ }second}}}$.
\end{problem}}%}

At a particular time, cyclist $A$ is ${42}$ ${\text{\texttt{hundred{ }meters}}}$ to the north of $P$ and traveling at ${8}$ ${\text{\texttt{meters{ }per{ }second}}}$, while cyclist $B$ is ${56}$ ${\text{\texttt{hundred{ }meters}}}$ to the east of $P$ and traveling at ${6}$ ${\text{\texttt{meters{ }per{ }second}}}$.  How fast is the distance between the two cyclists changing? \\[0.5in]

\input{Derivative-Compute-0031.HELP.tex}

The distance between the two cyclists is increasing by $\answer{\frac{48}{5}}$ ${\text{\texttt{meters{ }per{ }second}}}$.
\end{problem}}%}
